[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow was detected by AddressSanitizer in the Apple-specific [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note parsing routine of libexif. The error occurs when running the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_loader_fuzzer` harness with a malformed input, leading to a [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read in `strcmp`. The overflow is rooted in [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` and propagates through the EXIF data loading [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - AddressSanitizer reports a heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at address [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5020000000b2[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The overflow originates in `strcmp` when called by [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapple/exif-mnote-data-apple.[0m[1;92mc:240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The corrupt read is made against a buffer of size [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes, reading beyond its [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Heap-buffer-overflow in parsing EXIF maker-note data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mApple format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_loader_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m drives the error via [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Stack trace:  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - exif_mnote_data_apple_identify  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - interpret_maker_note [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-data.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-data.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - exif_loader_get_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-loader.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput [0m[1;39m([0m[39mharness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The faulty buffer is allocated with `calloc` in `exif_data_alloc` for [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note entries, but subsequently used in `strcmp` without ensuring sufficient [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. AddressSanitizer shadow output confirms the read occurs immediately past the [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m232[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m233[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m234[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Remove any old entries *[0m[35m/[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m235[0m[39m:    [0m[39mexif_mnote_data_canon_clear [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m238[0m[39m:    [0m[39mn->entries = exif_mem_alloc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mne->mem, sizeof [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteCanonEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m239[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!n->entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m240[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mEXIF_LOG_NO_MEMORY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mne->log, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteCanon"[0m[39m, sizeof [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mMnoteCanonEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m241[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m242[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m243[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m244[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Parse the entries *[0m[35m/[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m245[0m[39m:    [0m[39mtcount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m246[0m[39m:    [0m[39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = c, o = datao; i; --i, o += [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m247[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39msize_t s;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m248[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m249[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mmemset[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&n->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtcount[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteCanonEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m250[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mo,buf_size,[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.[0m[1;92mc:237[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m247[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m237:e[0m[1;35mxif_mnote_data_apple_identify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst ExifData *ed, const ExifEntry *e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m241[0m[39m:        variant = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m242[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m243[0m[39m:        variant = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m244[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m245[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m246[0m[39m:    return variant;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m247[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Apple-specific identify function `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally calls `[0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39me->data, [0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `e->data` points to a buffer allocated to exactly the tag’s data length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextra null terminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so if the buffer is shorter than the literal `[0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`strcmp` reads past the allocated region, causing a heap-buffer-overflow.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still want to detect the Apple maker-note when the payload begins with the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mASCII prefix `[0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m` and return variant `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`; otherwise, return `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter fuzzing harnesses, tests, or other maker-note handlers [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., Canon, Fuji[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch in `apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the body of `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m237[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m247[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe prefix-check.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Steps:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Define the expected prefix string and compute its length at compile time.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Early-out if the entry pointer, data pointer, or reported data length [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`e->size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is insufficient.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Use `memcmp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `strncmp`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m limited to the known prefix length—this avoids [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading past the end of `e->data`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d. Return `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` if the prefix matches, else `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Implementation Steps  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`, locate:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_apple_identify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst ExifData *ed, const ExifEntry *e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          int variant;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m e->data, [0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              variant = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              variant = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return variant;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace it with:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_apple_identify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst ExifData *ed, const ExifEntry *e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          const char apple_prefix[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          const size_t prefix_len = [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mapple_prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes *[0m[35m/[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Guard against NULL pointers and too-short data *[0m[35m/[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!e || !e->data || e->size < prefix_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Safe comparison: only compare prefix_len bytes *[0m[35m/[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmemcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[39me->data, apple_prefix, prefix_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure you include `<string.h>` at top of file [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Checking `e->size < prefix_len` guarantees we never read past the allocated [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `memcmp` compares exactly `prefix_len` bytes and does not rely on null [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminators in `e->data`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Behavior remains identical for valid Apple maker-notes starting with `[0m[32m"Apple [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32miOS"[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-Apple variants[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unaffected, tests and fuzz [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness logic unchanged.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If there was any reliance on a trailing null [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely, since subsequent Apple[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing operates on raw binary maker-note entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it is unchanged.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broader impact on other maker-note formats or generic EXIF parsing.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Additional Files or Harness Changes Required  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All modifications are localized to the Apple identify function in [0m             [2m                [0m
